\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_af6eeef78bb367ca17ab712839cfcc63e}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Write\+Frame\+Adjustment\+Reg}(Peripheral\+Base,  Value)

\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a3c9bad015f918fef1426402bc1ec0d10}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment}(Peripheral\+Base,  Value)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Sets frame adjustment. In Host mode, the frame adjustment is a twos complement number that adjusts the period of each U\+SB frame in 12-\/\+M\+Hz clock periods. A S\+OF is normally generated every 12,000 12-\/\+M\+Hz clock cycles. The \hyperlink{struct_frame}{Frame} Adjust Register can adjust this by -\/128 to +127 to compensate for inaccuracies in the U\+SB 48-\/\+M\+Hz clock. Changes to the A\+DJ bit take effect at the next start of the next frame. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_adec184ceccb0cfb9243177d3e1eab32a}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Read\+Clock\+Recovery\+Ctrl\+Reg}(Peripheral\+Base)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Returns the content of the Clock recovery control register. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a874c8483f07c9c3b48cb56e37547f3a1}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Write\+Clock\+Recovery\+Reg}(Peripheral\+Base,  Value)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Writes Value to the Clock recovery control register. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a6e866da38b3a1a596f42c14f393ea4ed}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Clock\+Recovery}(Peripheral\+Base,  \hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enables/disables clock recovery block. This block must be enabled if user wants to use the crystal-\/less U\+SB mode for the Full Speed U\+SB controller and transceiver. N\+O\+TE\+: This block should not be set for U\+SB host mode or O\+TG. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_accc5d7243cdf90376c5afbd73582537f}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase}(Peripheral\+Base,  \hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enables/disables reset/resume to rough phase. The clock recovery block tracks the I\+R\+C48\+Mhz to get an accurate 48\+Mhz clock. It has two phases after user enables clock\+\_\+recover\+\_\+en bit, rough phase and tracking phase. The step to fine tune the I\+RC 48\+Mhz by adjusting the trim fine value is different during these two phases. The step in rough phase is larger than that in tracking phase. Switch back to rough stage whenever U\+SB bus reset or bus resume occurs. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_ac8ff4d983fbf87a28ce16247adaf4c49}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Restart\+From\+I\+F\+R\+Trim\+Value}(Peripheral\+Base,  \hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enables/disables restart from I\+FR trim value. I\+R\+C48 has a default trim fine value whose default value is factory trimmed (the I\+FR trim value). Clock recover block tracks the accuracy of the clock 48\+Mhz and keeps updating the trim fine value accordingly. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a038d28dfbe64996711e5ec55018e675d}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Read\+I\+R\+C48\+M\+Oscillator\+Enable\+Reg}(Peripheral\+Base)

\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a6975571c2b983aaf4ca54cce640d9a7a}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Write\+I\+R\+C48\+M\+Oscillator\+Enable\+Reg}(Peripheral\+Base,  Value)

\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_aae2950dfeb60b804dee66e91bc427dc6}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+I\+R\+C48M}(Peripheral\+Base,  \hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enables/disables I\+R\+C48M module. This macro is used to enable the on-\/chip I\+R\+C48\+Mhz module to generate clocks for crystal-\/less U\+SB. It can only be used for FS U\+SB device mode operation. This module must be enabled before using the crystal-\/less U\+SB clock configuration. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \hyperlink{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_a7233ccb8bbceb668df956bcceee331e7}{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+I\+R\+C48\+M\+Regulator}(Peripheral\+Base,  \hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enables/disables I\+R\+C48M regulator. This macro is used to enable the the local analog regulator for I\+R\+C48\+Mhz module. This regulator must be enabled if user wants to use the crystal-\/less U\+SB clock configuration.. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

Enables/disables clock recovery block. This block must be enabled if user wants to use the crystal-\/less U\+SB mode for the Full Speed U\+SB controller and transceiver. N\+O\+TE\+: This block should not be set for U\+SB host mode or O\+TG.

\hline
{\em State} & Requested state. This parameter is of "Global enumeration used for specifying general enable/disable states (P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+LE and P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+LE defined in \hyperlink{_p_d_d___types_8h}{P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Types.\+h})" type. \\

Enables/disables I\+R\+C48M module. This macro is used to enable the on-\/chip I\+R\+C48\+Mhz module to generate clocks for crystal-\/less U\+SB. It can only be used for FS U\+SB device mode operation. This module must be enabled before using the crystal-\/less U\+SB clock configuration.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_accc5d7243cdf90376c5afbd73582537f}\label{_u_s_b___p_d_d_8h_accc5d7243cdf90376c5afbd73582537f}} 
\index{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h}!U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase}}
\index{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase}!U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase}{USB\_PDD\_EnableResetResumeToRoughPhase}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Reset\+Resume\+To\+Rough\+Phase(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{Peripheral\+Base,  }\item[{}]{\hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
( \(\backslash\)
    USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_REG(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)(( \(\backslash\)
      (uint8\_t)(( \(\backslash\)
       USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_REG(PeripheralBase)) & ( \(\backslash\)
       (uint8\_t)(~(uint8\_t)USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_RESET\_RESUME\_ROUGH\_EN\_MASK)))) | ( \(\backslash\)
      (uint8\_t)((uint8\_t)(\hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State}) << USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_RESET\_RESUME\_ROUGH\_EN\_SHIFT))) \(\backslash\)
  )
\end{DoxyCode}


Enables/disables reset/resume to rough phase. The clock recovery block tracks the I\+R\+C48\+Mhz to get an accurate 48\+Mhz clock. It has two phases after user enables clock\+\_\+recover\+\_\+en bit, rough phase and tracking phase. The step to fine tune the I\+RC 48\+Mhz by adjusting the trim fine value is different during these two phases. The step in rough phase is larger than that in tracking phase. Switch back to rough stage whenever U\+SB bus reset or bus resume occurs. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Restart\+From\+I\+F\+R\+Trim\+Value}{USB\_PDD\_EnableRestartFromIFRTrimValue}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Enable\+Restart\+From\+I\+F\+R\+Trim\+Value(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{Peripheral\+Base,  }\item[{}]{\hyperlink{group___x_f1__module_ga5d74787dedbc4e11c1ab15bf487e61f8}{State} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
( \(\backslash\)
    USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_REG(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)(( \(\backslash\)

       USB\_CLK\_RECOVER\_CTRL\_REG(PeripheralBase)) & ( \(\backslash\)

\end{DoxyCode}


Enables/disables restart from I\+FR trim value. I\+R\+C48 has a default trim fine value whose default value is factory trimmed (the I\+FR trim value). Clock recover block tracks the accuracy of the clock 48\+Mhz and keeps updating the trim fine value accordingly.

\index{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h}!U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment}}
\index{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment}!U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h@{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment}{USB\_PDD\_SetFrameAdjustment}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+S\+B\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+Frame\+Adjustment(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{Peripheral\+Base,  }\item[{}]{Value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
( \(\backslash\)
    USB\_USBFRMADJUST\_REG(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)(Value) \(\backslash\)
  )
\end{DoxyCode}


Sets frame adjustment. In Host mode, the frame adjustment is a twos complement number that adjusts the period of each U\+SB frame in 12-\/\+M\+Hz clock periods. A S\+OF is normally generated every 12,000 12-\/\+M\+Hz clock cycles. The \hyperlink{struct_frame}{Frame} Adjust Register can adjust this by -\/128 to +127 to compensate for inaccuracies in the U\+SB 48-\/\+M\+Hz clock. Changes to the A\+DJ bit take effect at the next start of the next frame. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline
{\em Value} & Value written to the \hyperlink{struct_frame}{Frame} adjustment register. This parameter is a 8-\/bit value. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a value of void type. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

The macro accesses the following registers\+: U\+S\+B0\+\_\+\+U\+S\+B\+F\+R\+M\+A\+D\+J\+U\+ST.
